! PING BLOCKER
! -------------------------------
! Ping Blocker ( Stop sites from tracking the links you visit through hyperlink auditing. )
! No need extension for that ( https://chrome.google.com/webstore/detail/ping-blocker/jkpocifanmihboebfhigkjcdihgfcdnb )
! Verify if ping requests (but also beacon api && csp report) are currently sent by your browser with Ping Spotter.
! < https://armin.dev/apps/ping-spotter >
!#if ping
*$ping
! [FIX] memory consumption too high
@@/player-events/log/partial$ping,domain=vimeo.com
! because "AdGuard Tracking Protection filter"
||vimeocdn.com/add/player-stats?beacon=$badfilter
@@/player-stats?beacon=$ping,domain=vimeo.com
!#endif
!#if xhr
! [fix] for those ping via xhr
! example "youboranqs01.com/ping"
/ping?$xhr,empty
!#endif
!

! Zuckestion concern
! Note 1: Some rules below are too long due to use an xpath, or multiple procedural chaining to make sure it won't accidentally
!         remove something that really need.
! Note 2: Inspired from report on https://github.com/collinbarrett/FilterLists/issues/282
! Proactive outbound tracking prevention, to prevent Facebook tracking you outside while click and open shared URL (see #19)
! Remark: If you're using uBlock0 or Nano, try click the magnifier icon to expand all parameters for getting real URL
||*&fbclid=$document,xmlhttprequest,important
||*?fbclid=$document,xmlhttprequest,important
||l.facebook.com$document,xmlhttprequest,important
